 pratyakshdarshiyon ne kaha, ek dhamaake kii aawaaj sunai di or arina ke duusari ore se jahaan se vah aawaaj ai thi, vahaan se log betahasha bhaagate hue hamaari ore aane lage

 britain network rail ne kaha ki manchester victoria stesan par trainon kii qatari lag gai thi

 manchester arina shahar kaa sabase bada indor venue he

 This is the second largest attack in the country after the fatal terrorist attack in London on 7 July 2005, in which a series of terrorist suicide bombings were carried out in Mandha Ladan
 hamale main vyast samay main saarvajanik parivahan pranali kaa istemaal kar aam logon ko nishaanaa banaaya gaya tha

 greater manchester ke aath aspataalon main unka ilaaj jari he

 unhone 1956 melbern or 1960 rome olympic main kramash: swarna or rajat padak jite the
 His family said that Bhola breathed his last on Monday
 unke parivaar main patni kamala bholaa, teen betiyaan or teen naati hai

 i pray for his soul's peace and my condolences to his family and the entire hockey world
 ’unhone kaha, ‘vah melbern main 1956 main olympic swarna ore rome main 1960 main olympic rajat padak jeetne vaali bhartiya purush hockey team ke sadsy the

 unhone 1954 se 1960 tak bhartiya vayusena or sena kii hockey tiimon kii captaini kii
